Multiple resource\\n27:   type URLs may be managed by a single muxer. CDS subscription mechanism is implemented in:\\n- **source/common/upstream/cds_api_impl.h/cc**: The main CDS API implementation (CdsApiImpl class) that subscribes to cluster discovery resources via the Subscription interface, handles onConfigUpdate callbacks, and manages cluster lifecycle.\\n- **source/common/upstream/cds_api_helper.h/cc**: Helper functions (CdsApiHelper class) that process cluster configuration updates and notify the ClusterManager about cluster changes.\\n- **source/common/upstream/od_cds_api_impl.h/cc**: On-demand CDS (OD-CDS) implementation for discovering clusters on-demand when traffic arrives for unknown clusters.\\n- **source/common/upstream/cluster_discovery_manager.h/cc**: Thread-local cluster discovery manager that handles on-demand cluster discovery callbacks and manages cluster lifecycle callbacks.\\n\\n## Cluster Manager Update Logic\\n\\nThe cluster manager update logic is located in:\\n- **source/common/upstream/cluster_manager_impl.h/cc**: Core ClusterManagerImpl class that receives cluster updates from CDS, manages cluster lifecycle (add/update/remove), handles thread-local cluster management, and coordinates updates across thread pools. Key methods include addOrUpdateCluster() which handles cluster configuration updates, and postThreadLocalClusterUpdate() which applies updates to thread-local instances.\\n- **source/common/upstream/cluster_update_tracker.h/cc**: Tracks cluster updates and notifies subscribers when clusters are added, updated, or removed.\\n- **source/common/upstream/cluster_factory_impl.h/cc**: Factory for creating cluster instances from configuration.\\n\\n## Health Check Scheduling and Execution\\n\\nThe active health check implementation is split across multiple files:\\n\\n**Base Health Check Implementation:**\\n- **source/extensions/health_checkers/common/health_checker_base_impl.h/cc**: Base HealthCheckerImplBase class that manages health check scheduling. Implements the ActiveHealthCheckSession class with interval timer and timeout timer management, handles health transitions, and manages callbacks.\\n\\n**Protocol-Specific Health Checkers:**\\n- **source/extensions/health_checkers/http/health_checker_impl.h/cc**: HTTP health check implementation (HttpHealthCheckerImpl) with HTTP request/response handling.\\n- **source/extensions/health_checkers/tcp/health_checker_impl.h/cc**: TCP health check implementation (TcpHealthCheckerImpl) with TCP connect verification.\\n- **source/extensions/health_checkers/grpc/health_checker_impl.h/cc**: gRPC health check implementation (GrpcHealthCheckerImpl) using the gRPC health check protocol.\\n- **source/extensions/health_checkers/redis/config.h/cc**: Redis health check implementation.\\n- **source/extensions/health_checkers/thrift/config.h/cc**: Thrift health check implementation.\\n\\n**Health Check Infrastructure:**\\n- **source/common/upstream/health_checker_impl.h/cc**: Factory (HealthCheckerFactory) and utility functions for creating health checker instances.\\n- **source/common/upstream/health_checker_event_logger.h/cc**: Event logging for health check events.\\n- **source/common/upstream/health_discovery_service.h/cc**: Health Discovery Service (HDS) that receives cluster health configurations from a management server.\\n\\n## Outlier Detection Integration\\n\\nThe outlier detection mechanism is implemented in:\\n- **source/common/upstream/outlier_detection_impl.h/cc**: Core outlier detection implementation including:\\n  - DetectorImpl: Main detector class that runs periodic checks (onIntervalTimer) to identify unhealthy hosts based on success rates, consecutive errors, etc.\\n  - DetectorHostMonitorImpl: Per-host monitor that tracks failure statistics and ejects/unejects hosts based on configured thresholds\\n  - DetectorConfig: Configuration parameters for ejection thresholds and detection criteria\\n  - EventLoggerImpl: Logs outlier detection events\\n\\nThe integration with health checking occurs through the putResult() method which receives health check outcomes and updates outlier detection statistics. The outlier detection system tracks consecutive failures, success rates, and can uneject hosts based on successful active health checks (via successful_active_health_check_uneject_host_ configuration).\\n\\n## Core Upstream Infrastructure\\n\\nSupporting infrastructure files:\\n- **source/common/upstream/upstream_impl.h/cc**: ClusterImplBase that owns and manages the health checker, delegates health check results to outlier detection, and tracks host health state.\\n- **source/common/upstream/host_utility.h/cc**: Utility functions for health flag management and serialization.\\n\\n## Architecture Flow\\n\\nThe complete flow is: CDS subscription -> cluster updates -> cluster manager adds/updates clusters -> health checker factory creates health checker instances -> health checker starts Active Health Check Sessions with interval timers -> health check results flow to outlier detection -> outlier detection ejects/unejects hosts based on configurable thresholds and can be influenced by active health check successes.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":4233,"cache_read_input_tokens":93621,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":4233},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"f6a86fa1-9a9f-4c05-8569-56a0ad7420f8","uuid":"7e17de03-e9b1-475f-9823-b17cb6e78904"}
